---
Title: ScottPlot Changelog
Description: Release log for every version of ScottPlot
Source: https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/blob/master/dev/changelog.md
---

## ScottPlot 4.1.37
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-03-25_
* Controls: Improved multi-axis support for mouse tracking by giving `GetMouseCoordinates()` optional axis index arguments ([#1743](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1743)) _Thanks [**@kv-gits**](https://github.com/kv-gits)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.36
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-03-19_
* Axis: Allow grid line and tick mark pixel snapping to be disabled ([#1721](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1721), [#1722](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1722)) _Thanks [**@Xerxes004**](https://github.com/Xerxes004)_
* Axis: `ResetLayout()` sets padding to original values to reverse changes made by adding colorbars ([#1732](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1732), [#1736](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1736)) _Thanks [**@ccopsey**](https://github.com/ccopsey)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.34
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-03-03_
* Bubble plot: Added methods to get the point nearest the cursor ([#1657](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1657), [#1652](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1652), [#1705](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1705)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX), [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233), and [**@adgriff2**](https://github.com/adgriff2)_
* Markers: Improved alignment of markers and lines on Linux and MacOS by half a pixel ([#1660](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1660), [#340](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/340))
* Plottable: Added `IsHighlighted` properties to make some plot types bold ([#1660](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1660)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Plottable: Segregated existing functionality interfaces for `IHasLine`, `IHasMarker`, and `IHilightable` ([#1660](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1660)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Plot: `AxisAuto()` now throws an exception of margins are defined outside the allowable range ([#450](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/450), [#1682](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1682)) _Thanks [**@xichaoqiang**](https://github.com/xichaoqiang)_
* Plot: Added `PlotFillRightLeft` method for adding horizontal filled scatter plots ([#450](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/450)) _Thanks [**@xichaoqiang**](https://github.com/xichaoqiang)_
* Markers: All shapes are now drawn discretely instead of relying on text rendering for improved performance and consistency ([#1668](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1668), [#1660](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1660)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Scatter Plot: Support distinct `LineColor` and `MarkerColor` colors ([#1668](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1668))
* SignalXY: Fix bug affecting the edge of the plot when step mode is active ([#1703](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1703), [#1699](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1699)) _Thanks [**@PeppermintKing**](https://github.com/PeppermintKing)_
* SignalXY: Improve appearance of filled regions when step mode is active ([#1703](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1703), [#1697](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1697)) _Thanks [**@PeppermintKing**](https://github.com/PeppermintKing)_
* Axis Span: Added options to customize fill pattern and border ([#1692](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1692)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Markers: Additional customization options such as `MarkerLineWidth` ([#1690](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1690)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Legend Viewer: New functionality to customize line, marker, and highlight options have been added to the the right-click menu of the Windows Forms control ([#1655](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1655), [#1651](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1651)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.33
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-02-04_
* Spline Interpolation: Added new methods for data smoothing including Bézier interpolation ([#1593](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1593), [#1606](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1606))
* Detachable Legend: Added an option to detach the legend to the right-click menu in the Windows Forms control. Clicking items in the detached legend toggles their visibility on the plot ([#1589](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1589), [#1573](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1573), [#1326](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1326)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Marker: Added an optional `Text` (and `TextFont`) for displaying a message that moves with a marker ([#1599](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1599))
* Heatmap: Heatmaps with custom X and Y sizing or positioning no longer call `AxisScaleLock()` automatically ([#1145](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1145)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Axis: GetCoordinateY() now returns more accurate coordinate ([#1625](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1625), [#1616](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1616)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Text: Now has `IsDraggable` field and improved mouseover detection that supports rotation ([#1616](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1616), [#1599](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1599)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX) and [**@Niravk1997**](https://github.com/Niravk1997)_
* Plot: `Frameless()` no longer results in an image with a 3 pixel transparent border ([#1571](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1571), [#1605](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1605)) _Thanks [**@sjlai1993**](https://github.com/sjlai1993)_
* Colorbar: `AddColorbar()` has new optional argument to enable placement on the left side of the plot ([#1524](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1524)) _Thanks [**@Niravk1997**](https://github.com/Niravk1997)_
* Heatmap: Fixed bug affecting manually-scaled heatmaps ([#1485](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1485)) _Thanks [**@ZPYin**](https://github.com/ZPYin), [**@mYcheng-95**](https://github.com/mYcheng-95), and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Colorbar: Exposed `DataAreaPadding` to improve layout customization for multi-axis plots ([#1637](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1637)) _Thanks [**@ccopsey**](https://github.com/ccopsey)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.32
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-01-23_
* Interpolation: New cubic interpolation module with improved stability and simplified API ([#1433](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1433)) _Thanks [**@allopatin**](https://github.com/allopatin)_
* Legend: `GetBitmap()` returns a transparent image instead of throwing an exception if there are no items in the legend ([#1578](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1578)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Legend: Added `Count`, `HasItems`, and `GetItems()` so users can inspect legend contents to if/how they want to display it ([#1578](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1578)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Plot: Exposed `GetDraggable()` to allow users to retrieve the plotted objects at specific pixel positions ([#1578](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1578)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Axis Limits: Improved handling of axis limits for plots containing no data ([#1581](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1581)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Repeating Axis Line: Improved display of text labels ([#1586](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1586), [#1557](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1557)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Axis: Improved multi-axis support for `GetPixel()` methods ([#1584](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1584), [#1587](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1587)) _Thanks [**@ChrisCC6**](https://github.com/ChrisCC6) and [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Error Bar: `Plot.AddErrorBars()` can now be used to place 1D or 2D error bars anywhere on the plot ([#1466](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1466), [#1588](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1588)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Scatter Plot List: Added generic support to `ScatterPlotList<T>` as demonstrated in the cookbook ([#1463](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1463), [#1592](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1592)) _Thanks [**@tyrbentsen**](https://github.com/tyrbentsen)_
* Draggable Scatter Plot: Created a new `ScatterPlotListDraggable` that supports dragging points and custom clamp logic as seen in the cookbook ([#1422](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1422)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru) and [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Axis: Users may now customize the number of minor ticks and grid lines when log scale is enabled ([#1594](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1594), [#1595](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1595), [#1583](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1583)) _Thanks [**@hibus**](https://github.com/hibus)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.31
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-01-17_
* MultiAxis: Improved support for draggable items placed on non-primary axes ([#1556](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1556), [#1545](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1545)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* RepeatingAxisLine: New plot types `RepeatingVLine` and `RepeatingHLine` show a primary line and a user-defined number of harmonics. See cookbook for example and usage notes. ([#1535](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1535), [#1775](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1775)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Scatter: The new `ScatterPlotDraggable` plot type is for creating scatter plots with mouse-draggable points ([#1560](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1560), [#1422](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1422)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX) and [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Controls: Improved middle-click-drag zoom rectangle support for plots with multiple axes ([#1559](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1559), [#1537](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1537)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Marker: New plot types `DraggableMarkerPlot` and `DraggableMarkerPlotInVector` give users options to add mouse-interactive markers to plots ([#1558](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1558)) _Thanks [**@BambOoxX**](https://github.com/BambOoxX)_
* Bar Plot: New `ValueFormatter` option allows users to customize the text displayed above bars ([#1542](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1542)) _Thanks [**@jankri**](https://github.com/jankri)_
* Plot: `Title()` now has additional arguments for customizing text above the plot ([#1564](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1564)) _Thanks Hendri_

## ScottPlot 4.1.30
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-01-15_
* Plot: Improve values returned by `GetDataLimits()` when axis lines and spans are in use ([#1415](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1415), [#1505](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1505), [#1532](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1532)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Rendering: Revert default text hinting from ClearType back to AntiAliased to improve text appearance on transparent backgrounds. Users may call `ScottPlot.Drawing.GDI.ClearType(true)` to opt-in to ClearType rendering which is superior for most situations. ([#1553](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1553), [#1550](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1550), [#1528](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1528)) _Thanks [**@r84r**](https://github.com/r84r), [**@wangyexiang**](https://github.com/wangyexiang), [**@Elgot**](https://github.com/Elgot), [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru), and [**@saklanmazozgur**](https://github.com/saklanmazozgur)_

<hr class='my-3' style='width: 50%; opacity: 0;'>


## ScottPlot 4.1.28
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2022-01-01_
* Eto Control: New ScottPlot control for the Eto GUI framework ([#1425](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1425), [#1438](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1438)) _Thanks [**@rafntor**](https://github.com/rafntor)_
* Radar Plot: `OutlineWidth` now allows customization of the line around radar plots ([#1426](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1426), [#1277](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1277)) _Thanks [**@Rayffer**](https://github.com/Rayffer)_
* Ticks: Improved minor tick and minor grid line placement ([#1420](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1420), [#1421](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1421)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann) and [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software)_
* Palette: Added Amber and Nero palettes ([#1411](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1411), [#1412](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1412)) _Thanks [**@gauravagrwal**](https://github.com/gauravagrwal)_
* Style: Hazel style ([#1414](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1414)) _Thanks [**@gauravagrwal**](https://github.com/gauravagrwal)_
* MarkerPlot: Improved data area clipping ([#1423](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1423), [#1459](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1459)) _Thanks [**@PremekTill**](https://github.com/PremekTill), [**@lucabat**](https://github.com/lucabat), and [**@AndXaf**](https://github.com/AndXaf)_
* MarkerPlot: Improved key in legend ([#1459](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1459), [#1454](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1454)) _Thanks [**@PremekTill**](https://github.com/PremekTill) and [**@Logicman111**](https://github.com/Logicman111)_
* Style: Plottables that implement `IStylable` are now styled when `Plot.Style()` is called. Styles are now improved for `ScaleBar` and `Colorbar` plot types. ([#1451](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1451), [#1447](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1447)) _Thanks [**@diluculo**](https://github.com/diluculo)_
* Population plot: Population plots `DataFormat` now have a `DataFormat` member that displays individual data points on top of a bar graph representing their mean and variance ([#1440](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1440)) Thanks _[**@Syntaxrabbit**](https://github.com/Syntaxrabbit)_
* SignalXY: Fixed bug affecting filled plots with zero area ([#1476](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1476), [#1477](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1477)) _Thanks [**@chenxuuu**](https://github.com/chenxuuu)_
* Cookbook: Added example showing how to place markers colored according to a colormap displayed in a colorbar ([#1461](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1461)) _Thanks [**@obnews**](https://github.com/obnews)_
* Ticks: Added option to invert tick mark direction ([#1489](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1489), [#1475](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1475)) _Thanks [**@wangyexiang**](https://github.com/wangyexiang)_
* FormsPlot: Improved support for WinForms 6 ([#1430](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1430), [#1483](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1483)) _Thanks [**@SuperDaveOsbourne**](https://github.com/SuperDaveOsbourne)_
* Axes: Fixed bug where `AxisAuto()` failed to adjust all axes in multi-axis plots ([#1497](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1497)) _Thanks [**@Niravk1997**](https://github.com/Niravk1997)_
* Radial Gauge Plot: Fixed bug affecting rendering of extremely small gauge angles ([#1492](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1492), [#1474](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1474)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
* Text plot and arrow plot: Now have `PixelOffsetX` and `PixelOffsetY` to facilitate small adjustments at render time ([#1392](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1392))
* Image: New `Scale` property allows customization of image size ([#1406](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1406))
* Axis: `Plot.GetDataLimits()` returns the boundaries of all data from all visible plottables regardless of the current axis limits ([#1415](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1415)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Rendering: Improved support for scaled plots when passing scale as a `Plot.Render()` argument ([#1416](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1416)) _Thanks [**@Andreas**](https://github.com/Andreas)_
* Text: Improved support for rotated text and background fills using custom alignments ([#1417](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1417), [#1516](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1516)) _Thanks [**@riquich**](https://github.com/riquich) and [**@AndXaf**](https://github.com/AndXaf)_
* Text: Added options for custom borders ([#1417](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1417), [#1516](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1516)) _Thanks [**@AndXaf**](https://github.com/AndXaf) and [**@MachineFossil**](https://github.com/MachineFossil)_
* Plot: New `RemoveAxis()` method allows users to remove axes placed by `AddAxis()` ([#1458](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1458)) _Thanks [**@gobikulandaisamy**](https://github.com/gobikulandaisamy)_
* Benchmark: `Plot.BenchmarkTimes()` now returns an array of recent frame render times ([#1493](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1493), [#1491](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1491)) _Thanks [**@anose001**](https://github.com/anose001)_
* Ticks: Disabling log-scaled minor ticks now disables tick label integer rounding ([#1419](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1419)) _Thanks [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software)_
* Rendering: Improve appearance of text by defaulting to ClearType font rendering ([#1496](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1496), [#823](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/823)) _Thanks [**@Elgot**](https://github.com/Elgot)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.27
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2021-10-24_
* Colorbar: Exposed fields for additional tick line and tick label customization ([#1360](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1360)) _Thanks [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233)_
* Plot: Improved `AxisAutoY()` margins ([#1363](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1363)) _Thanks [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233)_
* Radar Plot: `LineWidth` may now be customized ([#1277](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1277), [#1369](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1369)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Controls: Stretching due to display scaling can be disabled with `Configuration.DpiStretch` in WPF and Avalonia controls ([#1352](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1352), [#1364](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1364)) _Thanks [**@ktheijs**](https://github.com/ktheijs) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Axes: Improved support for log-distributed minor tick and grid lines ([#1386](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1386), [#1393](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1393)) _Thanks [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software)_
* Axes: `GetTicks()` can be used to get the tick positions and labels from the previous render
* WPF Control: Improved responsiveness while dragging with the mouse to pan or zoom ([#1387](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1387), [#1388](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1388)) _Thanks [**@jbuckmccready**](https://github.com/jbuckmccready)_
* Layout: `MatchLayout()` has improved alignment for plots containing colorbars ([#1338](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1338), [#1349](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1349), [#1351](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1351)) _Thanks [**@dhgigisoave**](https://github.com/dhgigisoave)_
* Axes: Added multi-axis support for `SetInnerViewLimits()` and `SetOuterViewLimits()` ([#1357](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1357), [#1361](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1361)) _Thanks [**@saroldhand**](https://github.com/saroldhand)_
* Axes: Created simplified overloads for `AxisAuto()` and `Margins()` that lack multi-axis arguments ([#1367](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1367)) _Thanks [**@cdytoby**](https://github.com/cdytoby)_
* Signal Plot: `FillAbove()`, `FillBelow()`, and `FillAboveAndBelow()` methods have been added to simplify configuration and reduce run-time errors. Direct access to fill-related fields has been deprecated. ([#1401](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1401))
* Plot: `AddFill()` now has an overload to fill between two Y curves with shared X values
* Palette: Made all `Palette` classes public ([#1394](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1394)) _Thanks [**@Terebi42**](https://github.com/Terebi42)_
* Colorbar: Added `AutomaticTicks()` to let the user further customize tick positions and labels ([#1403](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1403), [#1362](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1362)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Heatmap: Improved support for automatic tick placement in colorbars ([#1403](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1403), [#1362](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1362))
* Heatmap: Added `XMin`, `XMax`, `YMin`, and `YMax` to help configure placement and edge alignment ([#1405](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1405)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Coordinated Heatmap: This plot type has been deprecated now that the special functionality it provided is present in the standard `Heatmap` ([#1405](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1405))
* Marker: Created a new `Marker` class to simplify the marker API. Currently it is a pass-through for `MarkerShape` enumeration members.
* Plot: `AddMarker()` makes it easy to place a styled marker at an X/Y position on the plot. ([#1391](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1391))
* Plottable: `AddPoint()` now returns a `MarkerPlot` rather than a `ScatterPlot` with a single point ([#1407](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1407))
* Axis lines: Added `Min` and `Max` properties to terminate the line at a finite point ([#1390](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1390), [#1399](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1399)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.26
_Published on [NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages?q=scottplot) on 2021-10-12_
* SignalPlotYX: Improve support for step display ([#1342](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1342)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Heatmap: Improve automatic axis limit detection ([#1278](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1278)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Plot: Added `Margins()` to set default margins to use when `AxisAuto()` is called without arguments ([#1345](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1345))
* Heatmap: Deprecated `ShowAxisLabels` in favor of tight margins (see cookbook) ([#1278](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1278)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Histogram: Fixed bug affecting binning of values at the upper edge of the final bin ([#1348](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1348), [#1350](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1350)) _Thanks [**@jw-suh**](https://github.com/jw-suh)_
* NuGet: Packages have improved debug experience with SourceLink and snupkg format symbols ([#1285](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1285))

## ScottPlot 4.1.25
* Palette: `ScottPlot.Palette` has been created and cookbook recipes have been updated to use it. The module it replaces (`ScottPlot.Drawing.Palette`) will not be marked obsolete until ScottPlot 5. ([#1299](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1299), [#1304](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1304))
* Style: Refactored to use static classes instead of enumeration members ([#1299](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1299), [#1291](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1291))
* NuGet: Improved System.Drawing.Common dependencies in user control packages ([#1311](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1311), [#1310](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1310)) _Thanks [**@Kritner**](https://github.com/Kritner)_
* Avalonia Control: Now targets .NET 5 ([#1306](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1306), [#1309](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1309)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Plot: Fixed bug causing `GetPixel()` to return incorrect values for some axes ([#1329](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1329), [#1330](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1330)) _Thanks [**@riquich**](https://github.com/riquich)_
* New Palettes:
  * `ColorblindFriendly` modeled after [Wong 2011](https://www.nature.com/articles/nmeth.1618.pdf) ([#1312](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1312)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
  * `Dark` ([#1313](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1313)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
  * `DarkPastel` ([#1314](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1314)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
  * `Redness` ([#1322](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1322)) _Thanks [**@wbalbo**](https://github.com/wbalbo)_
  * `SummerSplash ([#1317](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1317))` _Thanks [**@KanishkKhurana**](https://github.com/KanishkKhurana)_
  * `Tsitsulin` 25-color optimal qualitative palette ([described here](http://tsitsul.in/blog/coloropt)) by [Anton Tsitsulin](http://tsitsul.in) ([#1318](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1318)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits) and [**@xgfs**](https://github.com/xgfs)_
* New Styles:
  * `Burgundy` ([#1319](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1319)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
  * `Earth` ([#1320](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1320)) _Thanks [**@martinkleppe**](https://github.com/martinkleppe)_
  * `Pink` ([#1234](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1234)) _Thanks [**@nanrod**](https://github.com/nanrod)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.23
* NuGet: use deterministic builds, add source link support, and include compiler flags ([#1285](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1285))

## ScottPlot 4.1.22
* Coxcomb Plots: Added support for image labels ([#1265](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1265), [#1275](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1275)) _Thanks [**@Rayffer**](https://github.com/Rayffer)_
* Palette: Added overloads for `GetColor()` and `GetColors()` to support transparency
* Plot Viewer: fixed bug causing render warning to appear in WinForms and Avalonia plot viewers ([#1265](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1265), [#1238](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1238)) _Thanks [**@bukkideme**](https://github.com/bukkideme), [**@Nexus452**](https://github.com/Nexus452), and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.21
* Legend: Throw an exception if `RenderLegend()` is called on a plot with no labeled plottables ([#1257](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1257))
* Radar: Improved support for category labels. ([#1261](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1261), [#1262](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1262)) _Thanks [**@Rayffer**](https://github.com/Rayffer)_
* Controls: Now have a `Refresh()` method as an alias of `Render()` for manually redrawing the plot and updating the image on the screen. Using `Render()` in user controls is more similar to similar plotting libraries and less likely to be confused with `Plot.Render()` in documentation and warning messages. ([#1264](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1264), [#1270](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1270), [#1263](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1263), [#1245](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1245), [#1165](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1165))
* Controls: Decreased visibility of the render warning (introduced in ScottPlot 4.1.19) by allowing it only to appear when the debugger is attached ([#1165](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1165), [#1264](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1264))
* Radial Gaugue Plot: Fixed divide-by-zero bug affecting normalized gauges ([#1272](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1272)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.18
* Ticks: Improve placement when axis scale lock is enabled ([#1229](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1229), [#1197](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1197))
* Plot: `SetViewLimits()` replaced by `SetOuterViewLimits()` and `SetInnerViewLimits()` ([#1197](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1197)) _Thanks [**@noob765**](https://github.com/noob765)_
* Plot: `EqualScaleMode` (an enumeration accepted by `AxisScaleLock()`) now has `PreserveSmallest` and `PreserveLargest` members to indicate which axis to prioritize when adjusting zoom level. The new default is `PreserveSmallest` which prevents data from falling off the edge of the plot when resizing. ([#1197](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1197)) _Thanks [**@noob765**](https://github.com/noob765)_
* Axis: Improved alignment of 90º rotated ticks ([#1194](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1194), [#1201](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1201)) _Thanks [**@gigios**](https://github.com/gigios)_
* Controls: Fix bug where middle-click-drag zoom rectangle would persist if combined with scroll wheel events ([#1226](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1226)) _Thanks [**@Elgot**](https://github.com/Elgot)_
* Scatter Plot: Fixed bug affecting plots where `YError` is set but `XError` is not ([#1237](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1237), [#1238](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1238)) _Thanks [**@simmdan**](https://github.com/simmdan)_
* Palette: Added `Microcharts` colorset ([#1235](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1235)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
* SignalPlotXY: Added support for `FillType` ([#1232](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1232)) _Thanks [**@ddrrrr**](https://github.com/ddrrrr)_
* Arrow: New plot type for rendering arrows on plots. Arrowhead functionality of scatter plots has been deprecated. ([#1241](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1241), [#1240](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1240))
* Controls: Automatic rendering has been deprecated. Users must call Render() manually at least once. ([#1165](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1165), [#1117](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1117))
* Radial Gauge Plots: `AddRadialGauge()` now adds a radial gauge plot (a new circular plot type where values are represented as arcs spanning a curve). See cookbook for examples and documentation. ([#1242](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1242)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.17
* Improved `RadarPlot.Update()` default arguments ([#1097](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1097)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
* Radar Plot: Improved `Update()` default arguments ([#1097](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1097)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
* Crosshair: Added `XLabelOnTop` and `YLabelOnRight` options to improve multi-axis support and label customization ([#1147](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1147)) _Thanks [**@rutkowskit**](https://github.com/rutkowskit)_
* Signal Plot: Added `StepDisplay` option to render signal plots as step plots when zoomed in ([#1092](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1092), [#1128](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1128)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Testing: Improved error reporting on failed XML documentation tests ([#1127](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1127)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Histogram: Marked `ScottPlot.Statistics.Histogram` obsolete in favor of static methods in `ScottPlot.Statistics.Common` designed to create histograms and probability function curves ([#1051](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1051), [#1166](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1166)). See cookbook for usage examples. _Thanks [**@breakwinz**](https://github.com/breakwinz) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* WpfPlot: Improve memory management for dynamically created and destroyed WpfPlot controls by properly unloading the dispatcher timer ([#1115](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1115), [#1117](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1117)) _Thanks [**@RamsayGit**](https://github.com/RamsayGit), [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann), [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg), and [**@Orace**](https://github.com/Orace)_
* Mouse Processing: Improved bug that affected fast drag-dropping of draggable objects ([#1076](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1076))
* Rendering: Fixed clipping bug that caused some plot types to be rendered above data area frames ([#1084](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1084))
* Plot: Added `Width` and `Height` properties
* Plot: `GetImageBytes()` now returns bytes for a PNG file for easier storage in cloud applications ([#1107](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1107))
* Axis: Added a `GetSettings()` method for developers, testers, and experimenters to gain access to experimental objects which are normally private for extreme customization
* Axis: Axis ticks now have a `Ticks()` overload which allows selective control over major tick lines and major tick labels separately ([#1118](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1118)) _Thanks [**@kegesch**](https://github.com/kegesch)_
* Plot: `AxisAuto()` now has `xAxisIndex` and `yAxisIndex` arguments to selectively adjust axes to fit data on a specified index ([#1123](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1123))
* Crosshair: Refactored to use two `AxisLine`s so custom formatters can now be used and lines can be independently styled ([#1173](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1173), [#1172](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1172), [#1122](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1122), 1195) _Thanks [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233) and [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* ClevelandDotPlot: Improve automatic axis limit detection ([#1185](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1185)) _Thanks [**@Nextra**](https://github.com/Nextra)_
* ScatterPlotList: Improved legend formatting ([#1190](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1190)) _Thanks [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233)_
* Plot: Added an optional argument to `Frameless()` to reverse its behavior and deprecated `Frame()` ([#1112](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1112), [#1192](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1192)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
* AxisLine: Added `PositionLabel` option for displaying position as text (using a user-customizable formatter function) on the axis ([#1122](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1122), [#1195](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1195), [#1172](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1172), [#1173](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1173)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru) and [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233)_
* Radar Plot: Fixed rendering artifact that occurred when axis maximum is zero ([#1139](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1139)) _Thanks [**@petersesztak**](https://github.com/petersesztak) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Mouse Processing: Improved panning behavior when view limits (axis boundaries) are active ([#1148](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1148), [#1203](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1203)) _Thanks [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software)_
* Signal Plot: Fixed bug causing render artifacts when using fill modes ([#1163](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1163), [#1205](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1205))
* Scatter Plot: Added support for `OffsetX` and `OffsetY` ([#1164](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1164), [#1213](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1213))
* Coxcomb: Added a new plot type for categorical data. See cookbook for examples. ([#1188](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1188)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Axes: Added `LockLimits()` to control pan/zoom manipulation so individual axes can be manipulated in multi-axis plots. See demo application for example. ([#1179](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1179), [#1210](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1210)) _Thanks [**@kkaiser41**](https://github.com/kkaiser41)_
* Vector Plot: Add additional options to customize arrowhead style and position. See cookbook for examples. ([#1202](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1202)) _Thanks [**@hhubschle**](https://github.com/hhubschle)_
* Finance Plot: Fixed bug affecting plots with no data points ([#1200](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1200)) _Thanks [**@Maoyao233**](https://github.com/Maoyao233)_
* Ticks: Improve display of rotated ticks on secondary axes ([#1201](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1201)) _Thanks [**@gigios**](https://github.com/gigios)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.16
* Made it easier to use custom color palettes (see cookbook) ([#1058](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1058), [#1082](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1082)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Added a `IgnoreAxisAuto` field to axis lines and spans ([#999](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/999)) _Thanks [**@kirsan31**](https://github.com/kirsan31)_
* Heatmaps now have a `Smooth` field which uses bicubic interpolation to display smooth heatmaps ([#1003](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1003)) _Thanks [**@xichaoqiang**](https://github.com/xichaoqiang)_
* Radar plots now have an `Update()` method for updating data values without clearing the plot ([#1086](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1086), [#1091](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1091)) _Thanks [**@arthurits**](https://github.com/arthurits)_
* Controls now automatically render after the list of plottables is modified (previously it was after the number of plottables changed). This behavior can be disabled by setting a public field in the control's `Configuration` module. ([#1087](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1087), [#1088](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1088)) _Thanks [**@bftrock**](https://github.com/bftrock)_
* New `Crosshair` plot type draws lines to highlight a point on the plot and labels their coordinates in the axes ([#999](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/999), [#1093](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1093)) _Thanks [**@kirsan31**](https://github.com/kirsan31)_
* Added support for a custom `Func<double, string>` to be used as custom tick label formatters (see cookbook) ([#926](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/926), [#1070](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1070)) _Thanks [**@damiandixon**](https://github.com/damiandixon) and [**@ssalsinha**](https://github.com/ssalsinha)_
* Added `Move`, `MoveFirst`, and `MoveLast` to the `Plot` module for added control over which plottables appear on top ([#1090](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1090)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)_
* Fixed bug preventing expected behavior when calling `AxisAutoX` and `AxisAutoY` ([#1089](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1089)) _Thanks [**@EFeru**](https://github.com/EFeru)__

<div>
<a href='https://github.com/arthurits'>

## ScottPlot 4.1.15
* Hide design-time error message component at run time to reduce flicking when resizing ([#1073](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1073), [#1075](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1075)) _Thanks [**@Superberti**](https://github.com/Superberti) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Added a modern `Plot.GetBitmap()` overload suitable for the new stateless rendering system (#913 [#1063](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1063))
* Controls now have `PlottableDragged` and `PlottableDropped` event handlers ([#1072](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1072)) _Thanks [**@JS-BGResearch**](https://github.com/JS-BGResearch)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.14
* Add support for custom linestyles in SignalXY plots ([#1017](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1017), [#1016](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1016)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg) and [**@breakwinz**](https://github.com/breakwinz)_
* Improved Avalonia dependency versioning ([#1018](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1018), [#1041](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1041)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Controls now properly process `MouseEnter` and `MouseLeave` events ([#999](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/999)) _Thanks [**@kirsan31**](https://github.com/kirsan31) and [**@breakwinz**](https://github.com/breakwinz)_
* Controls now have a `RenderRequest()` method that uses a render queue to facilitate non-blocking render calls ([#813](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/813), [#1034](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1034)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Added Last() to finance plots to make it easier to access the final OHLC ([#1038](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1038)) _Thanks [**@CalderWhite**](https://github.com/CalderWhite)_
* Controls that fail to render in design mode now display the error message in a textbox to prevent Visual Studio exceptions ([#1048](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1048)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.13-beta
* `Plot.Render()` and `Plot.SaveFig()` now have a `scale` argument to allow for the creation of high resolution scaled plots ([#983](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/983), [#982](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/982), [#981](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/981)) _Thanks [**@PeterDavidson**](https://github.com/PeterDavidson)_
* A `BubblePlot` has been added to allow display of circles with custom colors and sizes. See cookbook for examples. ([#984](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/984), [#973](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/973), [#960](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/960)) _Thanks [**@PeterDavidson**](https://github.com/PeterDavidson)_
* Avalonia 0.10.3 is now supported ([#986](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/986)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Default version of System.Drawing.Common has been changed from `5.0.0` to `4.6.1` to minimize errors associated with downgrading ([#1004](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1004), [#1005](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/1005), [#993](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/993), [#924](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/924), [#655](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/655)) _Thanks [**@bukkideme**](https://github.com/bukkideme)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.12-beta
* Added "Open in New Window" option to right-click menu ([#958](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/958), [#969](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/969)) _Thanks [**@ademkaya**](https://github.com/ademkaya) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* User control `Configuration` module now has customizable scroll wheel zoom fraction ([#940](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/940), [#937](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/937)) _Thanks [**@PassionateDeveloper86**](https://github.com/PassionateDeveloper86) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Added options to `Plot.AxisScaleLock()` to let the user define scaling behavior when the plot is resized ([#933](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/933), [#857](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/857)) _Thanks [**@ricecakebear**](https://github.com/ricecakebear) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved XML documentation for `DataGen` module ([#903](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/903), [#902](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/902)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Fixed bug where tick labels would not render for axes with a single tick ([#945](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/945), [#828](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/828), [#725](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/725), [#925](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/925)) _Thanks [**@saklanmazozgur**](https://github.com/saklanmazozgur) and [**@audun**](https://github.com/audun)_
* Added option to manually refine tick density ([#828](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/828)) _Thanks [**@ChrisAtVault**](https://github.com/ChrisAtVault) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Improved tick density calculations for DateTime axes ([#725](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/725)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Fixed SignalXY rendering artifact affecting the right edge of the plot ([#929](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/929), [#931](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/931)) _Thanks [**@damiandixon**](https://github.com/damiandixon) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved line style customization for signal plots ([#929](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/929), [#931](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/931)) _Thanks [**@damiandixon**](https://github.com/damiandixon) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Fixed bug where negative bar plots would default to red fill color ([#968](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/968), [#946](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/946)) _Thanks [**@pietcoussens**](https://github.com/pietcoussens)_
* Fixed bug where custom vertical margin was not respected when `AxisAuto()` was called with a middle-click ([#943](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/943)) _Thanks Andreas_
* Added a minimum distance the mouse must travel while click-dragging for the action to be considered a drag instead of a click ([#962](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/962))
* Improved Histogram documentation and simplified access to probability curves ([#930](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/930), [#932](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/932), [#971](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/971)) _Thanks [**@LB767**](https://github.com/LB767), [**@breakwinz**](https://github.com/breakwinz), and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.11-beta
* FormsPlot mouse events are now properly forwarded to the base control ([#892](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/892), [#919](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/919)) _Thanks [**@grabul**](https://github.com/grabul)_
* Prevent right-click menu from deploying after right-click-drag ([#891](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/891), [#917](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/917))
* Add offset support to SignalXY ([#894](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/894), [#890](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/890)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Eliminate rendering artifacts in SignalXY plots ([#893](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/893), [#889](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/889)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg) and [**@grabul**](https://github.com/grabul)_
* Optimize cookbook generation and test execution ([#901](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/901)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.10-beta
* Fixed a bug where applying the Seabourn style modified axis frame and minor tick distribution ([#866](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/866)) _Thanks [**@oszymczak**](https://github.com/oszymczak)_
* Improved XML documentation and error reporting for getting legend bitmaps ([#860](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/860)) _Thanks [**@mzemljak**](https://github.com/mzemljak)_
* Fixed rendering bug affecting finance plots with thin borders ([#837](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/837)) _Thanks [**@AlgoExecutor**](https://github.com/AlgoExecutor)_
* Improved argument names and XML docs for SMA and Bollinger band calculation methods ([#830](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/830)) _Thanks [**@ticool**](https://github.com/ticool)_
* Improved GetPointNearest support for generic signal plots ([#809](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/809), [#882](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/882), [#886](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/886)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg), [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software), and [**@mrradd**](https://github.com/mrradd)_
* Added support for custom slice label colors in pie charts ([#883](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/883), [#844](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/844)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann), [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg), and [**@Timothy343**](https://github.com/Timothy343)_
* Improved support for transparent heatmaps using nullable double arrays ([#849](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/849), [#852](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/852)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Deprecated bar plot `IsHorizontal` and `IsVertical` in favor of an `Orientation` enumeration
* Deprecated bar plot `xs` and `ys` in favor of `positions` and `values` which are better orientation-agnostic names
* Added Lollipop and Cleveland plots as new types of bar plots ([#842](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/842), [#817](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/817)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Fixed a bug where `Plot.AddBarGroups()` returned an array of nulls ([#839](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/839)) _Thanks [**@rhys-wootton**](https://github.com/rhys-wootton)_
* Fixed a bug affecting manual tick labels ([#829](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/829)) _Thanks [**@ohru131**](https://github.com/ohru131)_
* Implemented an optional render queue to allow asynchronous rendering in user controls ([#813](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/813)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.9-beta
* Improved support for negative DateTimes when using DateTime axis mode ([#806](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/806), [#807](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/807)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg) and [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software)_
* Improved axis limit detection when using tooltips ([#805](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/805), [#811](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/811)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann) and [**@ChrisAtVault**](https://github.com/ChrisAtVault)_
* Added `WickColor` field to candlestick plots ([#803](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/803)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Improved rendering of candlesticks that open and close at the same price ([#803](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/803), [#800](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/800)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann) and [**@AlgoExecutor**](https://github.com/AlgoExecutor)_
* Improved rendering of SignalXY plots near the edge of the plot ([#795](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/795)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* new `AddScatterStep()` helper method creates a scatter plot with the step style ([#808](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/808)) _Thanks [**@KlaskSkovby**](https://github.com/KlaskSkovby)_
* Marked `MultiPlot` obsolete
* Refactored `Colormap` module to use classes instead of reflection ([#767](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/767), [#773](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/773)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Refactored `OHLC` fields and finance plots to store `DateTime` and `TimeSpan` instead of `double` ([#795](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/795))

## ScottPlot 4.1.8-beta
* Improved validation and error reporting for large heatmaps ([#772](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/772)) _Thanks [**@Matthias-C**](https://github.com/Matthias-C)_
* Removed noisy console output in `ScatterPlotList` ([#780](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/780)) _Thanks [**@Scr0nch**](https://github.com/Scr0nch)_
* Improved rendering bug in signal plots ([#783](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/783), [#788](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/788)) _Thanks [**@AlgoExecutor**](https://github.com/AlgoExecutor) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Fix bug that hid grid lines in frameless plots ([#779](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/779))
* Improved appearance of marker-only scatter plots in the legend ([#790](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/790)) _Thanks [**@AlgoExecutor**](https://github.com/AlgoExecutor)_
* `AddPoint()` now has a `label` argument to match `AddScatter()` ([#787](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/787)) _Thanks [**@AlgoExecutor**](https://github.com/AlgoExecutor)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.7-beta
* Added support for image axis labels ([#759](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/759), [#446](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/446), [#716](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/716)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Added `MinRenderIndex` and `MaxRenderIndex` support to Scatter plots ([#737](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/737), [#763](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/763)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved display of horizontal manual axis tick labels ([#724](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/724), [#762](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/762)) _Thanks [**@inqb**](https://github.com/inqb) and [**@Saklut**](https://github.com/Saklut)_
* Added support for listing and retrieving colormaps by their names ([#767](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/767), [#773](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/773)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Enabled mouse pan and zoom for plots with infinitely small width and height ([#768](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/768), [#733](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/733), [#764](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/764)) _Thanks [**@saklanmazozgur**](https://github.com/saklanmazozgur)_
* A descriptive exception is now thrown when attempting to create heatmaps of unsupported dimensions ([#722](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/722)) _Thanks [**@Matthias-C**](https://github.com/Matthias-C)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.6-beta
* Fixed single point render bug in Signal plots ([#744](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/744), [#745](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/745)) _Thanks [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved display scaling support for WPF control ([#721](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/721), [#720](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/720)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* User control `OnAxesChanged` events now send the control itself as the sender object ([#743](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/743), [#756](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/756)) _Thanks [**@at2software**](https://github.com/at2software)_
* Fixed configuration bug related to Alt + middle-click-drag-zoom ([#741](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/741)) _Thanks [**@JS-BGResearch**](https://github.com/JS-BGResearch) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Fixed render bug related to ALT + middle-click-drag zoom box ([#742](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/742)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Fixed render bug for extremely small plots ([#735](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/735))
* Added a coordinated heatmap plot type ([#707](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/707)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved appearance of heatmap edges ([#713](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/713)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved design-time rendering of Windows Forms control
* Added and expanded XML documentation for Plot and Plottable classes
* Created a new cookbook website generator that combines reflection with XML documentation ([#727](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/727), [#738](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/738), [#756](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/756))
* ScottPlot is now a reserved prefix on NuGet

## ScottPlot 4.1.5-beta
* Helper methods were added for creating scatter plots with just lines (`AddScatterLines()`) or just markers (`AddScatterPoints()`).
* Scatter and Signal plots have `GetPointNearest()` which now has a `xyRatio` argument to support identifying points near the cursor in pixel space ([#709](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/709), [#722](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/722)) _Thanks [**@oszymczak**](https://github.com/oszymczak), [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg), [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Improved display of manual tick labels ([#724](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/724)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.1.4-beta
* User controls have been extensively redesigned ([#683](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/683))
  * All user controls are almost entirely logic-free and pass events to `ScottPlot.Control`, a shared common back-end module which handles mouse interaction and pixel/coordinate conversions.
  * Controls no longer have a `Configure()` method with numerous named arguments, but instead a `Configuration` field with XML-documented public fields to customize behavior.
  * Renders occur automatically when the number of plottables changes, meaning you do not have to manually call `Render()` when plotting data for the first time. This behavior can be disabled in the configuration.
  * Avalonia 0.10.0 is now supported and uses this new back-end ([#656](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/656), [#700](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/700)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
  * Events are used to provide custom right-click menu actions.
  * The right-click plot settings window (that was only available from the WinForms control) has been removed.
* New methods were added to `ScottPlot.Statistics.Common` which efficiently find the Nth smallest number, quartiles, or other quantiles from arrays of numbers ([#690](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/690)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* New tooltip plot type ([#696](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/696)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Fixed simple moving average (SMA) calculation ([#703](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/703)) _Thanks [**@Saklut**](https://github.com/Saklut)_
* Improved multi-axis rendering ([#706](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/706)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Improved `SetSourceAsync()` for segmented trees ([#705](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/705), [#692](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/692)) _Thanks [**@jl0pd**](https://github.com/jl0pd) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved layout for axes with rotated ticks ([#706](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/706), [#699](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/699)) _Thanks [**@MisterRedactus**](https://github.com/MisterRedactus) and [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* ScottPlot now multi-targets more platforms and supports the latest C# language version on modern platforms but restricts the language to C# 7.3 for .NET Framework projects ([#691](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/691), [#711](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/711)) _Thanks [**@jl0pd**](https://github.com/jl0pd)_
* Improved project file to install `System.ValueTuple` when targeting .NET Framework 4.6.1 ([#88](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/88), [#691](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/691))

## ScottPlot 4.1.0

In November, 2020 ScottPlot 4.0 branched into a permanent `stable` branch, and ScottPlot 4.1 began development as beta / pre-release in the main branch. ScottPlot 4.0 continues to be maintained, but modifications are aimed at small bugfixes rather than large refactoring or the addition of new features. ScottPlot 4.1 merged into the master branch in November, 2020 ([#605](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/605)). Improvements are focused at enhanced performance, improved thread safety, support for multiple axes, and options for data validation.

* **Most plotting methods are unchanged so many users will not experience any breaking changes.**
* **Axis Limits**
  * Axis limits are described by a `AxisLimits` struct (previously `double[]` was used)
  * Methods which modify axis limits do not return anything (previously they returned `double[]`)
  * To get the latest axis limits call `Plot.AxisLimits()` which returns a `AxisLimits` object
* **Multiple Axes**
  * Multiple axes are now supported! There is no change to the traditional workflow if this feature is not used.
  * Most axis methods accept a `xAxisIndex` and `yAxisIndex` arguments to specify which axes they will modify or return
  * Most plottable objects have `xAxisIndex` and `yAxisIndex` fields which specify which axes they will render on
  * You can enable a second Y and X axis by calling `YLabel2` and `XLabel2()`
  * You can obtain an axis by calling `GetXAxis(xAxisIndex)` or `GetYAxis(yAxisIndex)`, then modify its public fields to customize its behavior
  * The default axes (left and bottom) both use axis index `0`
  * The secondary axes (right and top) both use axis index `1`
  * You can create additional axes by calling `Plot.AddAxis()` and customize it by modifying fields of the `Axis` it returns.
* **Layout**
  * The layout is re-calculated on every render, so it automatically adjusts to accommodate axis labels and ticks.
  * To achieve extra space around the data area, call `Layout()` to supply a minimum size for each axis.
  * To achieve a frameless plot where the data area fills the full figure, call `LayoutFrameless()`
* **Some namespaces and class names have changed**
  * The `Plottable` base class has been replaced with an `IPlottable` interface
  * Plottables have been renamed and moved into a `Plottable` namespace (e.g., `PlottableScatter` is  now `Plottable.ScatterPlot`)
  * Several enums have been renamed
* **The Settings module has been greatly refactored**
  * It is still private, but you can request it with `Plot.GetSettings()`
  * Many of its objects implement `IRenderable`, so their customization options are stored at the same level as their render methods.
* **The Render system is now stateless**
  * `Bitmap` objects are never stored. The `Render()` method will create and return a new `Bitmap` when called, or will render onto an existing `Bitmap` if it is supplied as an argument. This allows controls to manage their own performance optimization by optionally re-using a `Bitmap` for multiple renders.
  * Drawing is achieved with `using` statements which respect all `IDisposable` drawing objects, improving thread safety and garbage collection performance.


<hr class='my-3' style='width: 50%; opacity: 0;'>

## ScottPlot 4.0.40
* Added user control for Avalonia ([#496](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/496), [#503](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/503)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Holding shift while left-click-dragging the edge of a span moves it instead of resizing it ([#509](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/509)) _Thanks [**@Torgano**](https://github.com/Torgano)_
* CSV export is now culture invariant for improved support on systems where commas are decimal separators ([#512](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/512)) _Thanks Daniel_
* Added fill support to scatter plots ([#529](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/529)) _Thanks [**@AlexFsmn**](https://github.com/AlexFsmn)_
* Fix bug that occurred when calling `GetLegendBitmap()` before the plot was rendered ([#527](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/527)) _Thanks [**@el-aasi**](https://github.com/el-aasi)_
* Improved DateTime tick placement and added support for milliseconds ([#539](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/539)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Pie charts now have an optional hollow center to produce donut plots ([#534](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/534)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann) and [**@AlexFsmn**](https://github.com/AlexFsmn)_
* Added electrocardiogram (ECG) simulator to the DataGen module ([#540](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/540)) _Thanks [**@AteCoder**](https://github.com/AteCoder)_
* Improved mouse scroll wheel responsiveness by delaying high quality render ([#545](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/545), [#543](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/543), [#550](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/550)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* `Plot.PlotBitmap()` allows Bitmaps to be placed at specific coordinates ([#528](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/528)) _Thanks [**@AlexFsmn**](https://github.com/AlexFsmn)_
* `DataGen.SampleImage()` returns a sample Bitmap that can be used for testing
* Bar graphs now have a hatchStyle property to customize fill pattern ([#555](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/555)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Support timecode tick labels ([#537](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/537)) _Thanks [**@vrdriver**](https://github.com/vrdriver) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_

## ScottPlot 4.0.39
* Legend now reflects LineStyle of Signal and SignalXY plots ([#488](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/488)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Improved mouse wheel zoom-to-cursor and middle-click-drag rectangle zoom in the WPF control for systems that use display scaling ([#490](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/490)) _Thanks [**@nashilnik**](https://github.com/nashilnik)_
* The `Configure()` method of user controls now has a `lowQualityAlways` argument to let the user easily enable/disable anti-aliasing at the control level. Previously this was only configurable by reaching into the control's plot object and calling its `AntiAlias()` method. ([#499](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/499)) _Thanks [**@RachamimYaakobov**](https://github.com/RachamimYaakobov)_
* SignalXY now supports parallel processing ([#500](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/500)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* SignalXY now respects index-based render limits ([#493](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/493), [#500](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/500)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg) and [**@envine**](https://github.com/envine)_

## ScottPlot 4.0.38
* Improved `Plot.PlotFillAboveBelow()` rendering of data with a non-zero baseline ([#477](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/477)) _Thanks [**@el-aasi**](https://github.com/el-aasi)_
* Added `Plot.PlotWaterfall()` for easy creation of waterfall-style bar plots ([#463](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/463), [#476](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/476)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Axis tick labels can be displayed using notations other than base 10 by supplying `Plot.Ticks()` with `base` and `prefix` arguments, allowing axes that display binary (e.g., `0b100110`) or hexadecimal (eg., `0x4B0D10`) tick labels ([#469](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/469), [#457](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/457)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Added options to `PlotBar()` to facilitate customization of text displayed above bars when `showValue` is enabled ([#483](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/483)) _Thanks [**@WillemWever**](https://github.com/WillemWever)_
* Plot objects are colored based on a pre-defined set of colors. The default colorset (category10) is the same palette of colors used by matplotlib. A new `Colorset` module has been created to better define this behavior, and `Plot.Colorset()` makes it easy to plot data using alternative colorsets. ([#481](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/481))
* Fixed a bug that caused instability when a population plot is zoomed-out so much that its fractional distribution curve is smaller than a single pixel ([#480](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/480)) _Thanks [**@HowardWhile**](https://github.com/HowardWhile)_
* Added `Plot.Remove()` method to make it easier to specifically remove an individual plottable after it has been plotted. `Plot.Clear()` is similar, but designed to remove classes of plot types rather than a specific plot object. ([#479](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/479)) _Thanks [**@cstyx**](https://github.com/cstyx) and [**@Resonanz**](https://github.com/Resonanz)_
* Signal plots can now be created with a defined `minRenderIndex` (in addition to the already-supported `maxRenderIndex`) to facilitate partial display of large arrays ([#474](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/474)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_

## ScottPlot 4.0.37
* Fixed a long-running issue related to strong assembly versioning that caused the WPF control to fail to render in the Visual Studio designer in .NET Framework (but not .NET Core) projects ([#473](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/473), [#466](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/466), [#356](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/356)) _Thanks [**@bhairav-thakkar**](https://github.com/bhairav-thakkar), [**@riquich**](https://github.com/riquich), [**@Helitune-RobMcKay**](https://github.com/Helitune-RobMcKay), and [**@iu2kxv**](https://github.com/iu2kxv)_
* User controls now also target `net472` (while still supporting `net461` and `netcoreapp3.0`) to produce a build folder with just 3 DLLs (compared to over 100 when building with .NET Framework 4.6.1)

## ScottPlot 4.0.36
* `PlotSignal()` and `PlotSignalXY()` plots now have an optional `useParallel` argument (and public property on the objects they return) to allow the user to decide whether parallel or sequential calculations will be performed. ([#454](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/454), [#419](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/419), [#245](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/245), [#72](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/72)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Improved minor tick alignment to prevent rare single-pixel artifacts ([#417](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/417))
* Improved horizontal axis tick label positions in ruler mode ([#453](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/453))
* Added a `Statistics.Interpolation` module to generate smooth interpolated splines from a small number of input data points. See advanced statistics cookbook example for usage information. ([#459](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/459)) _Thanks Hans-Peter Moser_
* Improved automatic axis adjustment when adding bar plots with negative values ([#461](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/461), [#462](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/462)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Created `Drawing.Colormaps` module which has over a dozen colormaps for easily converting a fractional value to a color for use in plotting or heatmap displays ([#457](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/457), [#458](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/458)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* Updated `Plot.Clear()` to accept any `Plottable` as an argument, and all `Plottable` objects of the same type will be cleared ([#464](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/464)) _Thanks [**@imka-code**](https://github.com/imka-code)_

## ScottPlot 4.0.35
* Added `processEvents` argument to `formsPlot2.Render()` to provide a performance enhancement when linking axes of two `FormsPlot` controls together (by calling `Plot.MatchAxis()` from the control's `AxesChanged` event, as seen in the _Linked Axes_ demo application) ([#451](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/451), [#452](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/452)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg) and [**@robokamran**](https://github.com/robokamran)_
* New `Plot.PlotVectorField()` method for displaying vector fields (sometimes called quiver plots) ([#438](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/438), [#439](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/439), [#440](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/440)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann) and [**@hhubschle**](https://github.com/hhubschle)_
* Included an experimental colormap module which is likely to evolve over subsequent releases ([#420](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/420), [#424](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/424), [#442](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/442)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* `PlotScatterHighlight()` was created as a type of scatter plot designed specifically for applications where "show value on hover" functionality is desired. Examples are both in the cookbook and WinForms and WPF demo applications. ([#415](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/415), [#414](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/414)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* `PlotRadar()` is a new plot type for creating Radar plots (also called spider plots or star plots). See cookbook and demo application for examples. ([#428](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/428), [#430](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/430)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* `PlotPlolygons()` is a new performance-optimized variant of `PlotPolygon()` designed for displaying large numbers of complex shapes ([#426](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/426)) _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* The WinForms control's `Configure()` now has a `showCoordinatesTooltip` argument to continuously display the position at the tip of the cursor as a tooltip ([#410](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/410)) _Thanks [**@jcbeppler**](https://github.com/jcbeppler)_
* User controls now use SHIFT (previously ALT) to lock the horizontal axis and ALT (previously SHIFT) while left-click-dragging for zoom-to-region. Holding CTRL+SHIFT while right-click-dragging now zooms evenly, without X/Y distortion. ([#436](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/436)) _Thanks [**@tomwimmenhove**](https://github.com/tomwimmenhove) and [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Parallel processing is now enabled by default. Performance improvements will be most noticeable on Signal plots. ([#419](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/419), [#245](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/245), [#72](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/72))
* `Plot.PlotBar()` now has an `autoAxis` argument (which defaults `true`) that automatically adjusts the axis limits so the base of the bar graphs touch the edge of the plot area. ([#406](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/406))
* OSX-specific DLLs are now only retrieved by NuGet on OSX ([#433](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/433), [#211](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/211), [#212](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/212))
* Pie charts can now be made with `plt.PlotPie()`. See cookbook and demo application for examples. ([#421](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/421), [#423](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/423)) _Thanks [**@bclehmann**](https://github.com/bclehmann)_
* `ScottPlot.FormsPlotViewer(Plot)` no longer resets the new window's plot to the default style ([#416](https://github.com/ScottPlot/ScottPlot/issues/416))  _Thanks [**@StendProg**](https://github.com/StendProg)_
* Controls now have a `recalculateLayoutOnMouseUp` option to prevent resetting of manually-defined data area padding
